</pre>
## Idea

A type is `π_n`-finite if it has finitely many connected components and all of its homotopy groups up to level `n` at all base points are finite.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="6633" class="Comment">-- Section 1. π-Finiteness</a>

<a id="6661" class="Comment">-- Definition 1.3</a>

<a id="6680" class="Comment">-- We introduce locally finite types</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-Prop"></a><a id="6718" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6718" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6741" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6745" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6746" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6746" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6750" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6755" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6759" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6762" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6746" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6764" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6766" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1322" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="6774" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6746" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="6776" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6718" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6799" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6799" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6801" class="Symbol">=</a>

            <a id="8581" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8583" href="foundation.propositions.html#1941" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8590" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8524" class="Bound">X</a>
              <a id="8606" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8608" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="8610" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8610" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8612" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8614" href="foundation.propositions.html#1941" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8621" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8524" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8623" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8626" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8626" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8628" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8630" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8371" class="Function">is-π-finite-Prop</a> <a id="8647" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8521" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8650" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="8653" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8610" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8655" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8626" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8656" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="9230" class="Comment">-- Basic properties of locally finite types</a>

<a id="9275" class="Comment">-- locally finite types are closed under equivalences</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv"></a><a id="9330" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9330" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9354" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9358" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9359" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9359" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9362" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9362" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9367" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9372" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9374" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9375" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9375" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9377" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9379" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9382" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9359" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9384" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9386" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9387" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9387" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9389" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9391" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9394" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9362" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9399" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9399" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9403" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9375" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9405" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9407" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9387" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9408" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9410" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9414" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6864" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9432" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9387" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9434" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9436" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6864" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9454" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9375" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9456" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9330" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9480" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9480" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9482" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9482" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9484" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9484" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9486" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9486" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9488" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="9492" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#6424" class="Function">is-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9510" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#16720" class="Function">equiv-ap</a> <a id="9519" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9480" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9521" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9484" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9523" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9486" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9527" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9482" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9530" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9540" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9480" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9542" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9484" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9543" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9546" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9556" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9480" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9558" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9486" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9559" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;"></a><a id="9563" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9563" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9588" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9593" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9593" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9596" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9596" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9601" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9606" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9608" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9609" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9609" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9613" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9616" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9593" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9618" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9620" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9621" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9621" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9625" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9628" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9596" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9630" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9633" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9633" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9635" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9637" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9609" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9639" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9641" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9621" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9642" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9644" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9648" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6864" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9666" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9609" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9668" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9670" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6864" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9688" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9621" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="9690" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9563" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9715" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9715" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9717" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9719" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9330" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9743" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9744" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5707" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="9754" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9715" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9755" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="9758" class="Comment">-- types with decidable equality are locally finite</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality"></a><a id="9811" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9811" class="Function">is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality</a> <a id="9852" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="18677" class="Comment">-- Dependent product of locally finite types</a>
